AARP Driver Safety Program

Provides 8-hour driver refresher course specially designed for drivers ages 50 and older, but open to people of any age. Class is intended to help older drivers improve their skills while teaching them to avoid accidents, traffic violations and learn adjustments to accommodate common age-related changes in vision, hearing, and reaction time. The class does not satisfy requirements for traffic violations, but may qualify partipants a discount on their auto insurance.Class locations and times vary, call for updated schedule. Online courses are also available. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308164

Animal Behavior Program

We offer classes for pets and their owners, and class registration is open to any dog or cat, including animals that were not adopted from the Houston SPCA. All classes are held one time per week and run for six weeks unless otherwise noted. Proper training and an understanding of animal behavior encourages responsible pet ownership and retention, and helps reduce relinquishment, abandonment and abuse. With thorough, consistent programs and activities, our animal behavior and training services can reduce knowledge deficits and have a strong, lasting impact on the bond between an individual and his or her pet. Last year, hundreds of pairs of pets and their owners received training through low cost classes, and thousands of people received free telephone counseling and email counseling which enabled us to address behavior issues immediately. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239461

Animal Exhibitions/Shows

Organizations that hold or otherwise enable people to participate in competitive events in which cats, dogs or other animals are posed or paraded or demonstrate the specific skills of their breed, and awards are given for the animals that best meet established criteria for excellence. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/991097

Animal Shelter

The Houston SPCA operates a high-quality, high-capacity shelter. We provide services to over 50,000 animals each year, primarily dogs, cats, rabbits, ferrets, small mammals, horses and farm animals. At our shelter, we typically receive owner-relinquished pets, injured strays and animals rescued from cruel and inhumane conditions. Occasionally, due to cruelty investigations rescues, we also house large and/or exotic animals, such as tigers, bears and chimpanzees. These animals are safely housed in a secure location at the shelter while we work to secure permanent placement at quality, AZA-accredited sanctuaries. The Houston SPCA shelter offers an open and welcoming environment to encourage potential adopters to get to know the many wonderful dogs, cats, birds and small mammals we have available. Horses and farm animals live on-site and at a satellite ranch facility. In an effort to provide care across a range of needs, our kennels come in varying sizes, to accommodate animals humanely, ensuring that they have enough space to walk, play and lie down without feeling cramped or overcrowded. Littermates and animals surrendered from the same home may be placed together for the animals’ comfort, but we never place more animals than can be accommodated into a single kennel. Animals are given enrichment toys, treats and beds, and all cats’ kennels have perches to climb on. Daily, all animals in the shelter receive care and socialization by our staff and volunteers, and dogs are taken on multiple walks. The Houston SPCA does not euthanize healthy, animals due to age, time limits or space. Once an animal is entered into the adoption program, he/she will only be euthanized if he/she develops a serious health or behavior issue. All animals are spayed or neutered prior to placement - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239459

Provides all potential new pet owners with counseling on responsible pet ownership and HSPCA policies on adoptions. The service tries to find quality homes for animals sheltered at the HSPCA. All adopters must fill out an application and meet with a counselor. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239460

Provides exhibits, reference services, and a meeting room. Offers tax forms. Participates in the TexShare program, a statewide consortium of libraries administered by the Texas State Library and Archives Commission. TexShare enables libraries across Texas to share print and electronic resources, including books, journals, technical reports, and databases. Choices

Christmas Eve Feast

Christmas Eve feast will take place Christmas Eve at the downtown George R. Brown Convention Center for anyone in need of a meal. Food baskets will be available to take home and prepare a meal on Christmas Day. A limited number of toys are available for children, however the child must be present at the event in order to receive a gift. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1379202

Chronic Disease and Injury Prevention Program

CIS - Aspire Even Start

Provides classes in GED, beginning or advanced ESL and parenting education to parents of young children (ages 0 - 7 r). Also provides early childhood education for children ages 2 months to 5 years, while parents attend English or GED classes. Participating families receive additional parenting education through home visits. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1318493

Citizen Police Academy

Provides a 12-week training program to educate community residents about the role of the police procedures. Speakers from various police deparment units present in their area of specialty and share their experiences. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308785

Citizenship Classes

Provides classes in U.S. civics and citizenship, guidance on the citizenship process, and financial assistance with citizenship application fees. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1241839

City of Austin - ADA Office

Ensures that City of Austin programs, services and facilities comply with the Americans with Disabilities Act. Individuals may contact the office to express concerns about any city service, such as: electric service, library, garbage pickup. Serves as a clearinghouse for information related to all disability laws, including: ADA, Fair Housing Act, Air Carriers Act, and parking laws. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305170

City of Austin - Bicycle and Pedestrian Program

Program works to improve and implement bicycle and pedestrian transportation facilities in the City of Austin. Includes working to create more bicycle lanes, wide curb lanes, trails, sidewalks, and crosswalks. Provides Austin bicycle maps for $5.00 - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304512

City of Austin - Child Safety Program

Provides crossing guards at all elementary schools within the City of Austin. Offers a free pedestrian/bike/bus safety training program in English and Spanish for City of Austin students in grades PreK-5th and children in day care. The program consists of a 45-minute interactive session conducted in the school gymnasium by two safety trainers. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1312944

City of Austin - City Hall/City Council

Serves as the administrative office for the City of Austin. Houses the Mayor's office, the City Council, City Manager's office, and other City offices. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304446

City of Austin - Equal Employment/Fair Housing Office (EE/FHO)

Provides investigation of any type of human rights or discrimination complaint, including but not limited to: complaints of employment and housing discrimination, complaints regarding unfair treatment from a business, the police, or the government, and complaints regarding denial of medical care. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305058

City of Austin - Human Resources Department

Accepts applications on-line for employment with the City of Austin; this main office does not serve the public on a walk-in basis. Visit one of the regional office locations to view City of Austin job listings, download and fill out an employment application, receive employment advice and counseling, attend employment seminars, and have access to online computer service. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305059

City of Austin Neighborhood Centers - Free School Supplies

Provides free school supplies by appointment while supplies last. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1436429

City of Austin - Neighborhood Housing and Community Development (NHCD) - Housing Services

Administers a variety of programs to serve the community's housing, community development and economic development needs. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304358

City of Austin NHCD - Lead Smart Program

The City of Austin's Lead Smart program is a free service that may assist with home repair for Austin and Travis County residents living in a home built before 1978 in order to make the home healthy and safe. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1455795

City of Austin Office of Homeland Security and Emergency Management - Disaster Ready Austin

Seeks to change the way Austin deals with disasters by taking preventative measures before disasters strike. Offers workshops and public education on disaster preparedness. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305892

City of Austin Office of Homeland Security and Emergency Management - Emergency Services

Coordinates services during county-wide emergencies, such as flooding, ice storms, and major power outages. Does not provide direct services to the public. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305890

City of Austin - Office of Sustainability

Briefs and advises the City of Austin regarding sustainability aspects of City policies, programs, and initiatives. Helps coordinate "green" and sustainable efforts and action for the City of Austin, provides community education and outreach, and manages the Austin Climate Protection Program. Housed within the City Manager's office. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304448

City of Austin - Office of the Police Monitor

Accepts complaints of misconduct against police officers and monitors investigations conducted by the Internal Affairs Division of the Austin Police Department. All matters are handled confidentially. Provides community outreach to educate and inform residents about the police department. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310284

City of Austin Parks and Recreation Department - Dougherty Arts Center Summer Camps

The Austin Parks and Recreation Department offers summer camps for children, ages 5 - 12 years, at the Dougherty Arts Center. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1316938

City of Austin PDRD - City Arborist Program

Provides assistance with development and tree preservation issues. Evaluates proposed development projects on a case-by-case and tree-by-tree basis. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304402

City of Austin PDRD - Code Compliance

Provides education and enforcement of city codes and ordinances. Investigates reports of code violations. Investigates reports of work being done without required city permits. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304396

City of Austin PDRD - Neighborhood Planning and Zoning Services

Provides planning, zoning, annexation, historic preservation, demographics, and design services. Offers the One Stop Shop, which provides consultation, review, and inspections for land development. Offers an opportunity for citizens to take an active role in the neighborhood planning process, where citizens, local stakeholders, city departments, community organizations and institutions work together to address land use planning and service delivery issues. Provides a Development Review process that development projects must follow so their design and construction meet community standards. Offers detailed information about neighborhood planning via website. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304392

City of Austin - Public Works and Transportation

Manages the City's Capital Improvement Program projects through all phases of design, construction, and inspection. Manages major road reconstruction projects, works on bicycle, pedestrian and urban trail projects-maintaining the City's network of roadways once they are built. Provides information on city transportation issues including street maintenance, traffic counts, traffic signal problems, missing or damaged traffic signs, parking enforcement, downtown parking meters and city projects. Call 311 to report obstructions in the driving lanes of roads and in alleys, potholes, other street repairs, and bridge repairs. Be ready to give exact location and type of obstruction. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304508

City of Austin - Transportation Department

Provides information for transportation services in the City of Austin. For traffic signals, streets signs, curb, crosswalk or school crossing guards problems call 311. Responsible for transportation planning and coordination, parking, special events and right of way management. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304408

Cleveland Office - DADS Adult Foster Care (AFC)

Adult Foster Care provides 24-hour living arrangement with supervision in an adult foster home for persons who, because of emotional, physical, or mental limitation, are unable to continue independent functioning in their own homes. Providers of AFC live in the household and share a common living area with individuals receiving services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428542

Cleveland Office - DADS Assisted Living/Residential Care (AL/RC)

Assisted living facilities and adult residential care homes provide 24-hour supervision and non-medical attendant care for adults with disabilities. Eligible clients do not require nursing home care. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428543

Cleveland Office - DADS Community Attendant Services (CAS)

Community Attendant Services (CAS) is a non-technical, non-skilled service providing in home attendant services to individuals with an approved medical need for assistance with personal care tasks. CAS is available to eligible adults and children whose health problems cause them to be functionally limited in performing activities of daily living according to practitioner’s statement of medical need. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428545

Cleveland Office - DADS Community Based Alternatives (CBA)

This program provides home- and community-based services to people who are elderly and to adults with disabilities as a cost-effective alternative to living in a nursing home. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. Services may be provided in a person's home or in a community-based living arrangement, such as a group home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1429151

Cleveland Office - DADS Community Living Assistance and Support Services (CLASS)

CLASS provides home- and community-based services to people with related conditions as a cost-effective alternative to placement in an intermediate care facility. This program is for individuals with an intellectual disability or a related condition (ICF/IID). A related condition is a disability, other than an intellectual disability, that originated before age 22 and that affects a person's ability to function in daily life. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428544

Cleveland Office - DADS Day Activity and Health Services (DAHS)

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428546

Cleveland Office - DADS Deaf Blind Multiple Disabilities Program (DBMD)

This Medicaid- waiver program provides home and community-based services to people who are deaf-blind with multiple disabilities, as a cost-effective alternative to institutional placement. The program focuses on increasing opportunities for consumers to communicate and interact with their environment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428547

Cleveland Office - DADS Emergency Response Services

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. In an emergency, the person can press a call button to signal for help. The electronic monitoring system helps to ensure that the appropriate person or service agency responds to an alarm call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428548

Cleveland Office - DADS Family Care (FC)

Family Care (FC) is a non-skilled, non-technical attendant care service available to eligible adults who are functionally limited in performing activities of daily living. Family Care services are provided by an attendant and do not require the supervision of a registered nurse. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428549

Cleveland Office - DADS Home-Delivered Meals (HDM)

The Home Delivered Meals program delivers at least one nutritious meal per day to individuals who are homebound and unable to prepare their own meals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428550

Cleveland Office - DADS Hospice Care

A program of relieving care at an individual’s place of residence consisting of medical, social, and support services to a terminally ill patient when curative treatment is no longer possible. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428551

Cleveland Office - DADS In Home and Family Support Services (IHFSP)

This program provides direct grant benefits to people who have physical disabilities, and/or to their families, to help them purchase services that enable them to live in the community. Participants choose and purchase services that help them to remain in their own homes. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428552

DFPS - Baby Moses Law Investigations

State law allows new mothers an alternative to newborn abandonment by designating emergency safe havens where they may leave their babies, ages newborn to 60 days. A safe haven is any hospital, fire rescue station, or emergency medical technician EMT in the state of Texas. A mother who chooses this option will not be prosecuted, as long as the baby is unharmed. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/988504

DHHS - Last Resort Communication Services

Provides sign language, oral interpreters, and real-time captioning for people who are deaf or hard of hearing to facilitate access to essential services and community participation. Program is available as a last resort only when the Americans with Disabilities Act and other access mandates are not applicable. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1439959

DHHS - Senior Citizen Program

Provides a means of bridging communication barriers and reducing isolation facing persons who are deaf or hard of hearing, ages 60 or older. Services vary from area to area and may include coping skills training, independent living services, and recreational activities. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1439964

DHHS - Specialized Telecommunications Assistance Program (STAP)

Provides financial assistance to persons with a disability to purchase specialized telecommunications equipment for access to telephone networks. Devices include: amplified telephones, two-way pagers, big button telephone, voice dialer, captioned telephone, and others. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1439957

Disaster Relief Services for Pets

The Houston SPCA is the leader in animal-related disaster response, rescue and recovery. Not only do we serve Houston and the surrounding area, but we also step in and extend our reach across the state, from the Mexican border to Louisiana, to respond to disasters and lend assistance to other shelters. When Hurricane Ike tore through the Gulf Coast in 2008, the Houston SPCA responded by standing up as the lead agency coordinating animal rescue and relief efforts, despite limited resources and a lack of power in the area. Through collaborated efforts between the Houston SPCA, other animal welfare agencies and volunteers from across the country, over 1,800 animal victims were rescued, cared for, and sheltered, including pets, horses and farm animals, and native wild babies displaced by the storm. Our rescue teams fielded 763 emergency requests to locate and rescue animals. Thanks to disaster relief efforts from the Houston SPCA and its supporters, many pets that were lost or left behind during the hurricane were able to return home, and displaced baby wild animalsparticularly squirrels and birdswere rehabilitated and released. The Houston SPCA serves as an active member on local and regional disaster task forces. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239463

DISCRIMINATORY TREATMENT AGAINST TRAVELERS

Provides assistance in resolving ""real time"" issues involving service animals, seating accommodations, enplaning, deplaning and connecting assistance, the stowage of personal equipment and other accommodations. Provides written information about your rights as an individual with a disability under the Air Carrier Access Act and 14 CFR Part 382. Offers information to help better plan your next air travel experience and information on how to resolve a disability-related dispute with an air carrier. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980174

Down Payment Assistance (DPA) Program

Provides qualified home buyers with a deferred, zero interest loan to assist with purchasing a home located within the Austin City limits. Assistance covers the down payment on a home and the eligible closing costs. Applicants must be able to qualify for a mortgage loan. Approved homes must be single-family homes, condos, or town homes, and the sales price must not exceed FHA limits. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304361

Downtown Austin Alliance (DAA)

Organization promotes the revitalization of Downtown Austin. Provides information about current economic developments and future plans, and co-sponsors events and speakers related to marketing the downtown area. Provides services and programs ensure that the Downtown neighborhood is safe, clean, accessible, and fun for residents, employees, and visitors. The Alliance is structured into four primary categories with supporting committees working to get things done. They are: Arts & Entertainment/Marketing, Parks, Streetscapes & Transportation, and Security & Maintenance. Call to request graffiti removal from the fronts and the sides of private property within the Downtown Public Improvement District.Provides the Downtown Development Packet that includes information on community demographics, parking, taxes, utility capability, and transportation alternatives. Compiles a retail/office vacancy chart for Downtown Austin that is available online. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1319655

Downtown Austin Community Court Services

Provides a community court for the City of Austin. Handles Class C misdemeanor, public order offenses such as public intoxication, possession of drug paraphernalia, disorderly conduct, simple assault, and aggressive panhandling that occur in the Downtown, East Austin, and West Campus areas within the City of Austin. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305559

Downtown Austin Rangers

The Rangers are citizen staff of the Austin Police Department. They do not carry weapons nor do they have the authority to make arrests. The purpose of the Rangers program is to enhance public safety by providing additional help to the Austin Police Department. Their visible presence in the Public Improvement District acts as a crime deterrent. The Rangers have the authority to request voluntary compliance for minor infractions of the law, such as public order violations. They also unlock vehicles free of charge in the downtown area.The Austin Police Department, the City of Austin, and the Austin Convention and Visitors Bureau provide formal training in safety patrol techniques and code enforcement, security issues, CPR/first aid, and community ambassadorship.The Rangers are a joint venture between the Downtown Austin Alliance and the Austin Police Department. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1319654

Services include tool loans, guidance and training. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308547

DPS - Aircheck Texas: Vehicle Registration, Inspection and Emissions Testing

All Texas registered vehicles are required to receive an annual inspection. Some counties require emissions testing also. Motorists have a 5-day grace period to get their inspection sticker. An inspection certificate expires on the last day of the month that is indicated on the windshield sticker. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321638

DPS - Help End Auto Theft (HEAT) Program

Helps law enforcement officers identify stolen vehicles. Any vehicle owner in Texas can obtain decals for his/her car or truck that authorizes law enforcement officers to stop the vehicle and verify ownership between 1:00 am and 5:00 am anywhere in Texas. Border decals are also available to alert officials to check ownership of any vehicle being driven across the border into Mexico. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981351

DPS - IdentoGO FAST Fingerprinting Services

Texas law authorizes fingerprint-based criminal history checks for designated volunteers and employment or licensing applicants. the Fingerprint Applicant Services of Texas (FAST) Program was developed to help Texans and their hosting agencies have fingerprinting applications processed more quickly. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1450578

DPS Paris - Driver License Services

Issues original and renewal driver permits, driver licenses, and Texas State Identification Cards. Processes change of address requests. Responds to requests for driving records and accident reports. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981373

DPS Paris - Texas Highway Patrol

Troopers are responsible for patrolling the highways to enforce traffic laws, issue citations to violators, investigate accidents, provide emergency first aid, assist disabled motorists, prevent or relieve traffic congestion, remove traffic obstructions, and perform other services that help to ensure that the highways are safe, convenient to use, and accident-free. To report a highway emergency or an erratic driver please have callers call 911. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981377

DPS Pflugerville - Driver License Services

Issues original and renewal driver permits, driver licenses, and Texas State Identification Cards. Processes change of address requests. Responds to requests for driving records and accident reports. Also issues Concealed Handgun Licenses. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1396382

DPS - Sex Offender Database

Provides a database that identifies convicted sex offenders in the state of Texas. Website also provides information about High-profile Fugitive Sex Offenders. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981389

DPS - Stranded/Disabled Motorist Helpline

Provides a statewide number for callers to report stranded cars and drunken drivers. Callers may also request non-emergency roadside assistance. To report traffic accidents, call 911. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981350

Issues original and renewal driver permits, driver licenses, and Texas State Identification Cards. Processes change of address requests. Responds to requests for driving records and accident reports. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981368

DPS Texarkana - Texas Highway Patrol

Troopers are responsible for patrolling the highways to enforce traffic laws, issue citations to violators, investigate accidents, provide emergency first aid, assist disabled motorists, prevent or relieve traffic congestion, remove traffic obstructions, and perform other services that help to ensure that the highways are safe, convenient to use, and accident-free. To report a highway emergency or an erratic driver please have callers call 911. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981362

DPS - Texas Amber Alert Network

Provides rapid notification of abducted child cases to the media and the public. Issues an emergency alert to television and radio stations within a 200-mile radius of the abduction once law enforcement is notified. State highway signs will flash warning messages to alert motorists. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981348

DPS - Texas Department of Emergency Management Shelter Hubs

Provides reception areas where people evacuating during a disaster may go for shelter registration and guidance. Evacuees may be transported from the shelter hubs to available beds at shelters. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321724

DPS - Texas Department of Emergency Management State Operations Center

Serves as the state warning point and primary state direction and control facility during emergency situations. It operates around the clock to monitor threats, provides information on emergency incidents to local, state, and federal officials and coordinates state emergency assistance to local governments. During major emergencies, state agencies and disaster service organizations convene at the SOC to identify, mobilize and deploy state and volunteer group resources to respond to emergencies. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321722

DPS - Texas Rangers

Provides investigation of major felony crimes, such as murder, rape, robbery, and burglary, as well as white-collar crimes and cases of governmental corruption. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981352

DPS - Veteran Driver's License Designation

Requires the Texas Department of Public Safety (DPS) to include a designation of "VETERAN" on the driver's licenses issued to eligible Veterans. This designation is a convenient way to provide proof of military status without having to produce a copy of form DD-214. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1334916

DPS - Victim Services Program

Provides direct and personal services to victims and their families throughout Texas. Also offers assistance in filling for Crime Victim's Compensation and evidence return, short-term counseling, personal advocacy and crisis intervention. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1269976

Drive a Senior - Northwest Austin

Provides volunteer support services for older adults living independently in their homes within boundaries in far northwest Austin, Cedar Park, and Leander. Services include free, personalized transportation and escort to medical appointments, shopping, and other errands, minor home repair and maintenance, and friendly visiting, telephone reassurance calls, and information and referral for older adult services. Staff visit clients' home for initial assessment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305099

Drive a Senior Northwest Austin - Loan Closet

Provides free loan of walkers, wheelchairs, toileting aids, crutches, shower seats, and other items on a short- or long-term basis for older adults living in far northwest Austin, Cedar Park, and Leander. Will take donations of equipment, but will not take hospital beds. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305111

Drive a Senior - West Austin

Provides volunteer support services for older adults living independently in their homes within boundaries in west Austin. Services include transportation to medical appointments and for errands, grocery shopping, friendly visiting, telephone reassurance calls, minor home repair and maintenance, information and referral for senior services, and case management. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305133

DRS - Comprehensive Rehabilitation Services (CRS) Program

Provides services for people who survive a traumatic injury to the spinal cord or brain to reenter their communities and live as independently as possible. Services include inpatient comprehensive medical rehabilitation; outpatient services, such as occupational, physical, speech and cognitive therapy; and post-traumatic brain injury services to help clients deal with injury-related cognitive difficulties such as memory loss and/or inappropriate behaviors. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1440957

DRS - Independent Living Services (ILS) Program

Contracts with local independent resource centers to provide services for people with disabilities to help them live more independently. Services include: counseling and guidance; training and tutorial services; adult basic education; rehabilitation facility training; telecommunications, sensory and other technological aids for people who are deaf; vehicle modification; assistive devices such as artificial limbs, braces, wheelchairs and hearing aids; and other services as needed to achieve independent living objectives, such as transportation, interpreter services and maintenance. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1440955

DSHS - Abstinence-Centered Education Program

Encourages the implementation of programs that aim to delay initiation of sexual activity in order to decrease the teen pregnancy rate and rate of sexually transmitted infections in youth ages 15 through 19. Project interventions focus on grades 5 – 12 with attention to factors that affect early initiation of sexual activity. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443272

DSHS - Abusable Volatile Chemicals Program (AVC)

Provides general information about abusable volatile chemicals, issuance and renewal applications for permits to sell abusable volatile chemicals, and permit information. Website features a free searchable database of license holders. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443809

DSHS - Adolescent Health

Provides adolescent health assessment training for registered nurses, physician's assistants, social workers, and nutritionists. The training is provided through the Texas Health Steps. Website provides health care information for teens, parents, and health care providers and a list of hotlines dealing with teen issues. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442994

DSHS - Adult Blood Lead Epidemiology and Surveillance Program (ABLES)

Investigates reports of adult lead poisoning cases for people ages 15 and older and maintains a surveillance database of adult blood lead test results for high risk groups. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442648

DSHS - Advisory Board of Athletic Trainers

Provides licensure and regulation of athletic trainers in Texas, and investigates complaints received about them. Website features a free searchable database of licensed athletic trainers, information about the profession and continuing education, and licensing and license renewal requirements and forms. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443663

DSHS - Alzheimer's Disease Program

Provides educational materials and information about Alzheimer's services for patients, caregivers, and healthcare professionals. Informs patients of any research projects and therapeutic trials open for their participation. Coordinates statewide planning and partner engagement. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443246

DSHS - Arthritis Program

Promotes arthritis prevention efforts, including self-evidence-based and self-management-based programs and health communication strategies, and monitors the prevalence of arthritis among Texans. Areas of focus include arthritis data and surveillance, health education and outreach, community policy and environmental change efforts, and clinical prevention and treatment. Promotes statewide planning to address the burden of arthritis in Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443265

DSHS - Asbestosis Surveillance Program

Maintains a database of information of cases of asbestosis in Texas. Website provides information about asbestosis symptoms, occupations at risk of developing the disease, and how to report cases. Asbestosis is a chronic fibrotic lung disease, which results from the long-term inhalation of respirable asbestos fibers. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442744

DSHS - Asbestos Program

Licenses workers engaged in asbestos-related activities, inspects reports of community asbestos exposure, and monitors asbestos removal in buildings. Website provides rosters of licensed asbestos professionals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443677

DSHS - Audiovisual Library

Lends free audiovisual material on health and safety education, early childhood intervention, and disability/rehabilitation topics to the public. Audiovisual material includes video, slide-tape, DVD, audio CD, and CD-ROM. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442970

DSHS - Bedding Program

Enforces the Texas Bedding Law through a program of licensing and statewide on-site inspections of manufacturing and processing facilities; germicidal treatment operations and retail outlets; and laboratory analysis of the contents and chemical treatment of bedding products. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1444331

DSHS - Birth and Death Records

Provides certified copies of Texas birth and death records, verification letters for births or deaths since 1903, amendments to birth or death certificates, apostilles (U.S. birth or death certificates prepared for foreign countries,) heirloom birth certificates, disinterment permits, and non-certified copies of original birth certificates for adult adoptees who were born in Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442524

DSHS - Birth Defects Epidemiology and Surveillance Branch

Maintains the Texas Birth Defects Registry, a birth defects surveillance system that collects information about infants and fetuses with birth defects born to women living in Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443094

DSHS - Breast and Cervical Cancer Services (BCCS)

Provides funding to local community health providers to offer breast and cervical cancer screening to eligible women. Services include breast examinations, mammograms, pap smears, colposcopies, biopsies, and cervical dysplasia treatment. Provides case and care management in addition to promoting public awareness and education. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442980

DSHS - Cardiovascular Disease and Stroke Program

Promotes and implements strategies to decrease risk factors for heart disease and prevent worsening of conditions for those with heart disease and stroke through improved treatment and healthier lifestyles. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443281

DSHS - Case Management for Children and Pregnant Women

Contracts with local providers to offer case management services for children with special health care needs and high-risk pregnant women. Program is an extension of Medicaid. Assists in accessing medical services, equipment and supplies, and in handling family problems, educational/school issues, and financial concerns. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442326

DSHS - Central Adoption Registry

Provides a voluntary mutual-consent registry that reunites adult adoptees, birth parents, or siblings. A match occurs when an adopted person and his or her birth parent or a biological sibling voluntarily registers and completes several prerequisites including a one-hour post-adoption counseling session that educates and prepares each for the reunion, a written biography or history about the participant's life with copies of photographs or other visual media, and provides consent to be contacted. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442543

DSHS - Child and Adolescent Mental Health and Substance Abuse Services

Funds providers of mental health and substance abuse services who then assist children and adolescents in need of such services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1444432

DSHS - Childhood Lead Poisoning Prevention Program (TX CLPPP)

Works toward the elimination of childhood lead poisoning in Texas through outreach, education, surveillance and environmental investigations. Maintains a surveillance system of blood lead results on children younger than 15 years of age. Website contains information about lead poisoning for the public. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442651

DSHS - Children with Special Health Care Needs Program (CSHCN)

Provides health benefits for children with special health care needs, their families, and people of all ages with cystic fibrosis. Contracts with agencies throughout the state to provide clinical and support services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442347

DSHS - Clearinghouse: Best Practices of Mental Health Systems

Helps Local Mental Health Authorities and other behavioral health providers, consumers, family members and interested stakeholders find information about effective approaches for improving mental health service systems, especially in Texas. Individuals may submit, suggest, and access best practices on website. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1445282

DSHS - Code Enforcement Officer Registration

Provides registration and regulation of code enforcement officers, and investigates complaints received about them. Website features a free searchable database of code enforcement officers, information about the profession and continuing education, and licensing and license renewal requirements and forms. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443661

DSHS - College Vaccine Requirements

Provides information about the required meningitis vaccine for incoming college and university students. Acts as resource to help students navigate meningococcal vaccine requirements. Lists requirements, how to obtain the vaccine, information about proof of vaccination, disease information, and exemptions. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443435

DSHS - Community Mental Health Centers

Provide mental health services, intellectual and developmental disability services, and substance abuse services in a designated service area. In most local service areas the designated Local Mental Health Authority (LMHA)and community mental health center are the same entity and provide both authority functions and services except in the NorthStar service area. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1445320

DSHS - Contact Lens Dispensing Permit Program

Provides registration and regulation of opticians who sell or dispense contact lenses, and investigates complaints received about them. Website features a free searchable database of permit holders, information about the profession and continuing education, and licensing and license renewal requirements and forms. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443654

DSHS - Contract and Development Support Branch

Provides contract development and support for the following DSHS contracted health services: - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442557

DSHS - Council on Sex Offender Treatment

Administers the outpatient sexually violent predatory program, licenses and maintains a list of licensed sex offender treatment providers, provides referrals to licensed sex offender treatment programs, establishes the rules and regulations regarding the treatment of sex offenders, and disseminates information to the public regarding the management of sex offenders. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443644

DSHS - County Indigent Health Care Program

Administers county indigent health care programs (CIHCP) in Texas. Hospital districts and public hospitals are required to provide basic health care services to their indigent residents. Counties that are not fully served by a hospital district or a public hospital are responsible for administering an indigent health care program for indigent residents. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442328

DSHS - Critical Incident Stress Management (CISM)

Provides crisis intervention to emergency service personnel, including dispatchers, who have experienced a critical incident in the line of duty. Critical Incident Stress Management CISM teams are available on a 24-hour basis to provide crisis intervention services and help emergency responders return to work. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443841

DSHS - Drinking Water Testing

Performs drinking water testing for the presence or absence of coliforms and E. coli bacteria. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443465

DSHS - Drugs and Medical Devices Division

Provides licensure and regulation of manufacturers, distributors and retailers of human and animal drugs, biological products, medical devices, cosmetics, indoor tanning studios, and tattoo and body piercing studios to ensure that they are safe and effective for their intended use, properly labeled, and free of harmful additives or contaminants. Investigates complaints received about licensees. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443760

DSHS - Dyslexia Therapist and Dyslexia Practitioner Licensing Program

Licenses and regulates dyslexia therapists and dyslexia practitioners in Texas. The website contains licensing requirements, how to file a complaint, continuing education information, and a searchable listing of dyslexia therapists and dyslexia practitioners in Texas. Online renewal available. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443668

DSHS - Emerging and Acute Infectious Disease Branch

Develops and conducts communicable disease surveillance activities to track trends in disease occurrence and to detect new and emerging diseases. Responds to inquiries from the public and medical communities regarding the occurrence, prevention, and control of communicable diseases. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442450

DSHS - EMS/Trauma Registry

Collects, analyzes, and disseminates information on the occurrence of major trauma in Texas, including spinal cord injuries, traumatic brain injuries, and submersion injuries. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443938

DSHS - EMS-Trauma Systems

Responsible for regional trauma system development and trauma facility designation across Texas. Responsible for the following programs: - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1444453

DSHS - Environmental Epidemiology and Health Studies Program

Conducts special health surveillance and investigations of non-communicable disease clusters, and epidemiological studies of non-communicable disease. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1445121

DSHS - Environmental Lead Program

Provides certification and regulation of people conducting lead-based paint activities in target housing and child-occupied facilities to ensure they are properly trained and are following minimum standards that protect the health of workers and building occupants. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443740

DSHS - Epilepsy Program

Contracts with service providers to offer comprehensive outpatient care for eligible people who have epilepsy and/or seizure-like symptoms. Services include case management, diagnosis and treatment of the medical condition, integration of personal, social and vocational support services, and public awareness and educational services. Program office provides list of contracted agencies, technical information for agencies, and information about epilepsy. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442988

DSHS - Exclusions from Immunization Requirements

Provides information about applying for an exemption from child-care and school immunization requirements. Parents/guardians may request an exemption for their child due to medical contraindications, reasons of conscience, including a religious belief, and active duty with the armed forces of the United States. Each individual vaccine exemption lasts for 2 years. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1446165

DSHS - Family Planning Program

Facilitates statewide delivery of preventive health care services to low-income women and men in Texas. Services are provided through public health regional clinics and through contracts with organizations such as local health departments, medical schools, hospitals, private non-profit agencies, and community health centers. Services include the following: - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442351

DSHS - Food Establishments Group

Provides licensure, regulation, and inspection of food establishments, retail food stores, mobile food units, and roadside vendors in areas of the state not under the jurisdiction of a local health authority. Investigates complaints received about these establishments. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443787

DSHS - Foods Group

Ensures the safety of all foods manufactured, processed, and/or distributed within the state of Texas, proper and truthful labeling, and that only wholesome food products are introduced into commerce. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443783

DSHS - Funding Information Center

Provides information on health-related funding opportunities available from public and private sources to Texas residents and organizations. Provides a free, online Funding Alert Grant Database. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442972

DSHS - Genetic Services

Provides information about genetics and genetic services including who should seek out services. Includes a list of genetic service providers that are available to Texas residents with family incomes at or less than 185% of the most current Federal Poverty Income Level (FPIL) who are not eligible for other programs providing the same services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442558

DSHS - Glenda Dawson Donate Life-Texas Registry

Provides a statewide internet-based registry of potential organ donors and educates the public about the benefits of organ, tissue, and eye donation. Texas residents can register their intent to be an organ, eye, and tissue donor when they renew their driver's license or personal identification card, or by visiting the website. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442989

DSHS - Hansen's Disease Program

Contracts with local health departments and Texas Centers for Infectious Disease of provide treatment to people diagnosed with Hansen's Disease. Clinics are located in Dallas, San Antonio, Harlingen, and Houston. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442659

DSHS - Hazardous Products

Licenses and regulates product manufacturers and retailers. Performs routine product inspections and investigates consumer complaints and injury related to consumer products. Consumer products regulated by this department include automotive products, household cleaners, polishes and waxes, paints and glues, infant items, children's toys, and sleep wear. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443737

DSHS - Health Assessment and Toxicology Program (HAT)

Assesses the potential health effects that exposure to toxic substances or harmful physical agents may have on people. Identifies potentially exposed communities, assesses how hazardous a site is, and recommends actions. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1444446

DSHS - Health Facility Program

Develops rules and grants licenses for health facilities; collects applications and architectural review fees; provides administrative support to the Texas Medical Disclosure Panel and responds to open record requests. Maintains a list of licensed facilities. Receives and investigates complaints of substandard care against the following regulated health care facilities: - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443492

DSHS - Health Professions Resource Center

Collects, analyzes, and disseminates data concerning the supply trends, geographical distribution, and demographics of health care professionals. Studies health care workforce issues and prepares reports on the findings. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443181

DSHS - Hemophilia Assistance Program

Provides financial assistance for blood products for eligible people with hemophilia. Individuals may apply to Hemophilia Assistance Program (HAP) year-round. Current clients must renew their applications before August 31 each year. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442263

DSHS - HIV/STD Program

Provides HIV and STD education, prevention counseling, screening and testing, partner elicitation and notification, and the provision of medical and social services mostly through contracted community agencies. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1446023

DSHS - Hospital Data Collection and Reporting

Collects and reports hospital facility information and hospital charity care data based on the Annual Survey of Hospitals and the Annual Statement of Community Benefits. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1444342

DSHS - IMMTRAC Texas Immunization Registry

Consolidates and stores immunization information electronically in one centralized system. Authorized professionals such as doctors, nurses, and public health providers can access clients’ vaccination histories. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443351

DSHS - Kidney Health Care Program

Provides limited financial assistance to Texas residents with end stage renal disease ESRD who have been approved to receive benefits. Primary benefits include payment for covered ESRD-related medical services including dialysis, payment for allowable drugs, travel for ESRD-related services, and Medicare premium payment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442298

DSHS - Licensed Chemical Dependency Counselor Program

Provides licensure and regulation of licensed chemical dependency counselors (LCDC), and investigates complaints received about them. Website features a free searchable database of licensed chemical dependency counselors, information about the profession and continuing education, and licensing and license renewal requirements and forms. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443640

DSHS - Literature and Forms Department

Provides free health-related literature and forms. Some materials are available in Spanish. Website provides online searching and ordering of all materials. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443349

DSHS - Marriage and Divorce Records

Provides verification letters stating whether or not a marriage or divorce was recorded with the State of Texas. Verification letters are not considered legal substitutes for marriage licenses or divorce decrees. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442542

DSHS - Massage Therapy Licensing Program

Provides licensure and regulation of massage therapists, massage therapy instructors, massage schools, and massage establishments in Texas, and investigates complaints received about them. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443637

DSHS - Meat Safety Assurance Unit

Provides regulation and inspection of meat and poultry facilities to ensure that meat and poultry products contain no harmful ingredients and are truthfully labeled, and that they are produced from healthy animals that are slaughtered humanely and prepared in a sanitary manner. Investigates complaints received about meat and poultry facilities. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443751

DSHS - Medical and Research Library

Provides a lending library containing health-related books, journals, and government documents. Loans out books only to employees of the Texas Department of State Health Services (DSHS) and Department of Assistive and Rehabilitative Services (DARS). Non-employees may visit the library and view the resource materials. Website provides a free, searchable online catalog of library materials. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442973

DSHS - Medical Radiologic Technologist Certification Program

Provides licensure and regulation of medical radiologic technologists in Texas, and investigates complaints received about them. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443631

DSHS - Mental Health and Substance Abuse Client Rights

Provides consultation on consumer rights and program issues within the Texas Department of State Health Services, Community Mental Health and Substance Abuse programs. Responds to general inquiries and investigates complaints regarding mental health and substance abuse facility patient treatment in Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442551

DSHS - Mental Health and Substance Abuse Information Center

Provides mental health and substance abuse prevention and treatment research materials. Books and videos may be checked out for a 2-week period. Curricula, journals, and reference documents must be used within the information center only. Mails materials to people living outside of Austin. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442553

DSHS - Milk Group

Ensure milk sanitarians have the resources, training, and supplies they need to do their work. Regulates and inspects dairy farms, milk processing plants, and haulers. Approves locations and plans for construction of dairy and processing facilities. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443745

DSHS - Mold Program

Licenses mold assessment and remediation professionals and companies, and investigates complaints about mold violations made by these entities. Accredits mold training providers and inspects mold remediation projects. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443678

DSHS - Newborn Screening Program

Provides newborn testing, follow-up, and clinical care coordination. All babies born in Texas are required to have two screens for 29 inheritable and other disorders. An abnormal laboratory results trigger follow-up and - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442327

DSHS - Occupational Health Indicators

Compiles and reports data from a state-based occupational condition surveillance system. Provides occupational indicator education materials. An occupational health indicator is a specific measurement of a work-related disease or injury. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1444450

DSHS - Offender Education Program

Provides certification and regulation of four types of court-ordered offender education programs: drug offender education programs, DWI education programs, DWI intervention programs, and alcohol education programs for minors also called Minor in Possession Programs, or MIP. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443623

DSHS - Opticians' Registry

Provides registration and regulation of opticians in Texas, and investigates complaints received about them. Website features a free searchable database of registered opticians, information about the profession, registration and registration renewal requirements and forms, and information about continuing education. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1443602

DSHS - Oral Health Program

Coordinates efforts to improve oral health of Texans and to prevent dental disease. Coordinates Texas Health Steps dental checkups. Program is designed to help school-age children with low income receive preventive dental services. Services are provided by public health dentists, hygienists and other partners. Website lists provided services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1442634

Earned Income Tax Credit - EITC

Provides a refundable, lump-sum federal tax credit for eligible working single people and families who earn below certain income levels. Galveston Office, Avenue S 1/2 - DFPS Kinship Program

Provides support for relatives and fictive kin, known as kinship caregivers, who accept placement in their home of children who are in the legal custody of the Texas Department of Family and Protective Services (DFPS) due to abuse or neglect. Provides eligible kinship caregivers with training and support groups, case management, information and referral services, family counseling, child care, assistance with application for public benefits, and in some cases, limited financial assistance. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1434000

Galveston Office - DADS Adult Foster Care (AFC)

Adult Foster Care provides 24-hour living arrangement with supervision in an adult foster home for persons who, because of emotional, physical, or mental limitation, are unable to continue independent functioning in their own homes. Providers of AFC live in the household and share a common living area with individuals receiving services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428596

Galveston Office - DADS Assisted Living/Residential Care (AL/RC)

Assisted living facilities and adult residential care homes provide 24-hour supervision and non-medical attendant care for adults with disabilities. Eligible clients do not require nursing home care. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428597

Galveston Office - DADS Community Attendant Services (CAS)

Community Attendant Services (CAS) is a non-technical, non-skilled service providing in home attendant services to individuals with an approved medical need for assistance with personal care tasks. CAS is available to eligible adults and children whose health problems cause them to be functionally limited in performing activities of daily living according to practitioner’s statement of medical need. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428599

Galveston Office - DADS Community Based Alternatives (CBA)

This program provides home- and community-based services to people who are elderly and to adults with disabilities as a cost-effective alternative to living in a nursing home. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. Services may be provided in a person's home or in a community-based living arrangement, such as a group home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1429158

Galveston Office - DADS Community Living Assistance and Support Services (CLASS)

CLASS provides home- and community-based services to people with related conditions as a cost-effective alternative to placement in an intermediate care facility. This program is for individuals with an intellectual disability or a related condition (ICF/IID). A related condition is a disability, other than an intellectual disability, that originated before age 22 and that affects a person's ability to function in daily life. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428598

Galveston Office - DADS Day Activity and Health Services (DAHS)

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428600

Galveston Office - DADS Deaf Blind Multiple Disabilities Program (DBMD)

This Medicaid- waiver program provides home and community-based services to people who are deaf-blind with multiple disabilities, as a cost-effective alternative to institutional placement. The program focuses on increasing opportunities for consumers to communicate and interact with their environment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428602

Galveston Office - DADS Emergency Response Services

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. In an emergency, the person can press a call button to signal for help. The electronic monitoring system helps to ensure that the appropriate person or service agency responds to an alarm call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428601

Galveston Office - DADS Family Care (FC)

Family Care (FC) is a non-skilled, non-technical attendant care service available to eligible adults who are functionally limited in performing activities of daily living. Family Care services are provided by an attendant and do not require the supervision of a registered nurse. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428603

Galveston Office - DADS Home-Delivered Meals (HDM)

The Home Delivered Meals program delivers at least one nutritious meal per day to individuals who are homebound and unable to prepare their own meals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428604

Galveston Office - DADS Hospice Care

A program of relieving care at an individual’s place of residence consisting of medical, social, and support services to a terminally ill patient when curative treatment is no longer possible. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428605

Galveston Office - DADS In Home and Family Support Services (IHFSP)

HHSC OSS - Adult Medicaid

Provides medical benefits for eligible low-income adults. Medicaid recipients will receive a plastic Your Texas Benefits Medicaid ID Card. Most Medicaid-approved medical services are free. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1441704

HHSC OSS - Children's Medicaid

Offers free health care services to children. Medicaid recipients will receive a plastic Your Texas Benefits Medicaid ID Card. Provides six months of coverage. Newborns receive 12 months of coverage if the mother was receiving Medicaid when the child was born. Coverage begins as soon as the application is approved. Before the end of each six-month period of coverage, a renewal application is sent to the family. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1441703

HHSC OSS - Medical Transportation Program (MTP)

Provides transportation assistance to adults and children enrolled in Medicaid, or in the Children with Special Health Care Needs program. Provides transportation to Medicaid related services, such as doctor's office, or for some clients: dentist office, hospital, or drug store. Assistance also includes bus passes and gasoline payment assistance. Medicaid may reimburse someone else to drive you to your doctor's visit or drug store if the driver meets certain requirements (see 'Helpful Tips'). - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1441707

HHSC OSS - Medicare Savings Program

Provides payment assistance for Medicare premiums, co-insurance and deductibles for eligible Medicare recipients. The benefit period for Medicare Savings Programs is usually one year. Annual reviews of eligibility are required. A redetermination form will be sent to that person, or his or her authorized representative prior to the review due date. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1441708

HHSC OSS - One Time Temporary Assistance to Needy Families (TANF)

Provides $1,000 in cash assistance for families in crisis. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1441697

HHSC OSS - Supplemental Nutrition Assistance Program (SNAP)

HHSC OSS - Temporary Assistance to Needy Families (TANF)

Provides financial help for children and their parents or relatives who are living with them. Families who are approved for TANF will receive payments for six months. HHSC will send a renewal application to the family before the end of the six months. Families who receive TANF benefits can also apply for Medicaid benefits. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1441696

HHSC OSS - Temporary Assistance to Needy Families (TANF) Annual School Subsidy

Provides an annual school subsidy payment of $30 for each TANF-eligible child in August. Payments are intended for clothing, school supplies, and other items children might need. The benefit is not restricted to school-age children. The extra payment is included in clients' August TANF electronic benefit transfer (EBT).The extra funds do not affect clients' TANF or food stamp benefits or Medicaid eligibility, and clients do not need to report them to their Texas Works Advisor. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1441699

HHSC OSS - Texas Medicaid Wellness Program

Provides grants and loans to units of local governments, nonprofit agencies, for-profit entities, and public housing agencies for the provision of safe, decent, affordable housing to low-income households. Eligible HOME Activities include:1. Homebuyer Assistance Program HBA provides down payment and closing cost assistance to eligible homebuyers for the acquisition of affordable single family housing including funds for accessibility modifications if required. The HBA Program also includes a Contract for Deed Conversion Program which provides funds for the purpose of converting an eligible Contract for Deed to homeownership and bringing the unit up to standards. This program includes set-aside funds for persons with disabilities, 2. Homeowner Rehabilitation Program provides funds for the rehabilitation and or reconstruction of single family homes, includes set-aside funds for persons with disabilities, includes a rehabilitation and refinance component. 3. Tenant Based Rental Assistance Program provides rental assistance, which may include security and utility deposits, tenants must participate in a self-sufficiency program, includes set-aside funds for persons with disabilities. 4. Rental Development Program provides funds for acquisition, new construction, and/or rehabilitation of multi-family rental property. 5. Single Family Development provides Community Housing Development Organizations CHDO, funds for the development of single family housing for affordable homeownership. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980351

This program is for individuals with an intellectual disability or a related condition (ICF/IID). A related condition is a disability, other than an intellectual disability, that originated before age 22 and that affects a person's ability to function in daily life. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428611

Houston Office, 40th St - DADS Day Activity and Health Services (DAHS)

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428613

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. In an emergency, the person can press a call button to signal for help. The electronic monitoring system helps to ensure that the appropriate person or service agency responds to an alarm call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428615

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428625

Houston Office, Fuqua St - DADS Deaf Blind Multiple Disabilities Program (DBMD)

This Medicaid- waiver program provides home and community-based services to people who are deaf-blind with multiple disabilities, as a cost-effective alternative to institutional placement. The program focuses on increasing opportunities for consumers to communicate and interact with their environment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428626

Houston Office, Fuqua St - DADS Emergency Response Services

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. In an emergency, the person can press a call button to signal for help. The electronic monitoring system helps to ensure that the appropriate person or service agency responds to an alarm call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428640

Houston Office, Fuqua St - DADS Family Care (FC)

Family Care (FC) is a non-skilled, non-technical attendant care service available to eligible adults who are functionally limited in performing activities of daily living. Family Care services are provided by an attendant and do not require the supervision of a registered nurse. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428628

Houston Office, Fuqua St - DADS Home-Delivered Meals (HDM)

The Home Delivered Meals program delivers at least one nutritious meal per day to individuals who are homebound and unable to prepare their own meals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428642

Houston Office, Fuqua St - DADS Hospice Care

A program of relieving care at an individual’s place of residence consisting of medical, social, and support services to a terminally ill patient when curative treatment is no longer possible. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428630

Participants choose and purchase services that help them to remain in their own homes. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428644

Houston Office, Harwin Dr - DADS Adult Foster Care (AFC)

Houston Office, Harwin Dr - DADS Client Managed Personal Assistance Services (CMPAS)

Health-related tasks are prescribed by physician. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428509

Humane Education Services

The Houston SPCAs Humane Education Department offers a range of age-appropriate activities for children from 2nd grade through 12th grade, with in-school animal welfare lessons and discussions, Critter Camp and the Paw Pals Girl Scout Patch Program. Offered twelve weeks throughout the year, Critter Camp is an unforgettable week long day camp experience that offers children a chance to learn about animals, the environment, pet ownership and future animal-related careers through fun and creative activities and hands-on interaction with animals. Aside from a nominal fee for Critter Camp enrollment, all of the Houston SPCA Humane Education programs are offered as a free service to the community, so that children can access quality, age-appropriate humane education regardless of their economic status. Our programs are engaging, hands-on and easily adaptable, so that we can provide services to a wide and diverse range of children, including those with physical and mental disabilities. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239465

ITIN

An Individual Taxpayer Identification Number ITIN is a tax processing number issued by the Internal Revenue Service. It is a nine-digit number that always begins with the number 9. The IRS issues ITINs to individuals who are required to have a U.S. taxpayer identification number but who do not have and are not eligible to obtain a Social Security Number SSN. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239786
