Liberty Office - DADS Adult Foster Care (AFC)

Adult Foster Care provides 24-hour living arrangement with supervision in an adult foster home for persons who, because of emotional, physical, or mental limitation, are unable to continue independent functioning in their own homes. Providers of AFC live in the household and share a common living area with individuals receiving services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428686

Liberty Office - DADS Assisted Living/Residential Care (AL/RC)

Assisted living facilities and adult residential care homes provide 24-hour supervision and non-medical attendant care for adults with disabilities. Eligible clients do not require nursing home care. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428687

Liberty Office - DADS Community Attendant Services (CAS)

Community Attendant Services (CAS) is a non-technical, non-skilled service providing in home attendant services to individuals with an approved medical need for assistance with personal care tasks. CAS is available to eligible adults and children whose health problems cause them to be functionally limited in performing activities of daily living according to practitioner’s statement of medical need. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428689

Liberty Office - DADS Community Based Alternatives (CBA)

This program provides home- and community-based services to people who are elderly and to adults with disabilities as a cost-effective alternative to living in a nursing home. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. Services may be provided in a person's home or in a community-based living arrangement, such as a group home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1429164

Liberty Office - DADS Community Living Assistance and Support Services (CLASS)

CLASS provides home- and community-based services to people with related conditions as a cost-effective alternative to placement in an intermediate care facility. This program is for individuals with an intellectual disability or a related condition (ICF/IID). A related condition is a disability, other than an intellectual disability, that originated before age 22 and that affects a person's ability to function in daily life. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428688

Liberty Office - DADS Day Activity and Health Services (DAHS)

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428690

Liberty Office - DADS Deaf Blind Multiple Disabilities Program (DBMD)

This Medicaid- waiver program provides home and community-based services to people who are deaf-blind with multiple disabilities, as a cost-effective alternative to institutional placement. The program focuses on increasing opportunities for consumers to communicate and interact with their environment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428691

Liberty Office - DADS Emergency Response Services

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. In an emergency, the person can press a call button to signal for help. The electronic monitoring system helps to ensure that the appropriate person or service agency responds to an alarm call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428692

Liberty Office - DADS Family Care (FC)

Family Care (FC) is a non-skilled, non-technical attendant care service available to eligible adults who are functionally limited in performing activities of daily living. Family Care services are provided by an attendant and do not require the supervision of a registered nurse. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428693

Liberty Office - DADS Home-Delivered Meals (HDM)

The Home Delivered Meals program delivers at least one nutritious meal per day to individuals who are homebound and unable to prepare their own meals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428694

Liberty Office - DADS Hospice Care

A program of relieving care at an individual’s place of residence consisting of medical, social, and support services to a terminally ill patient when curative treatment is no longer possible. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428695

Liberty Office - DADS In Home and Family Support Services (IHFSP)

This program provides direct grant benefits to people who have physical disabilities, and/or to their families, to help them purchase services that enable them to live in the community. Participants choose and purchase services that help them to remain in their own homes. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428696

Liberty Office - DADS Medically Dependent Children Program (MDCP)

The program provides services to support families caring for children and young adults who are medically dependent and to encourage de-institutionalization of children in nursing facilities. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428697

Liberty Office - DADS Primary Home Care (PHC)

This program is a nontechnical, medically-related personal care service provided to adults whose health problems cause them to be functionally limited in performing activities of daily living, according to a statement of medical need. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428698

Liberty Office - DFPS Kinship Program

Provides support for relatives and fictive kin, known as kinship caregivers, who accept placement in their home of children who are in the legal custody of the Texas Department of Family and Protective Services (DFPS) due to abuse or neglect. Provides eligible kinship caregivers with training and support groups, case management, information and referral services, family counseling, child care, assistance with application for public benefits, and in some cases, limited financial assistance. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1434034

Library Services

Provides public library services including print, large-print, multilingual, and audiovisual materials for checkout, reference materials, meeting space, and public access to computers with Internet and word processing access. Offers children's library services, including story time and programs for youth. Offers materials for the study of English and United States Citizenship. Provides tax forms and computer classes. Many branches offer adult book groups. Many branches provide test proctoring services, call for more information.Participates in the TexShare program, a statewide consortium of libraries administered by the Texas State Library and Archives Commission. TexShare enables libraries across Texas to share print and electronic resources, including books, journals, technical reports, and databases. Texans in good standing at their local library may obtain a free TexShare card, enabling them to borrow items at other libraries throughout Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1309486

Library Services

Provides public library services including print, large-print, multilingual, and audiovisual materials for checkout, reference materials, meeting space, and public access to computers with Internet and word processing access. Offers children's library services, including story time and programs for youth. Offers materials for the study of English and United States Citizenship. Provides tax forms and computer classes. Many branches offer adult book groups. Many branches provide test proctoring services, call for more information.Participates in the TexShare program, a statewide consortium of libraries administered by the Texas State Library and Archives Commission. TexShare enables libraries across Texas to share print and electronic resources, including books, journals, technical reports, and databases. Texans in good standing at their local library may obtain a free TexShare card, enabling them to borrow items at other libraries throughout Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1309632

Listen, Look and Learn

Provides a presentation that explains speech/language deficits experienced in the elderly by examining a comprehensive model, describes the breakdowns which occur in deficits, such as expressive vs. receptive aphasia, dysarthia, apraxia, and various types of dementia, provides suggestions based on therapeutic techniques in how to communicate, depending upon the deficit, and illustrates how these deficits relate to swallowing problems. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1255430

Literacy Council of Williamson County - Literacy and Tutoring Services

Provides tutoring in English as a Second Language (ESL), GED and basic adult literacy for adults with low literacy skills and/or who do not have a high school diploma. Adults learn to read, write and speak English. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308062

Little Walnut Creek Library - Victory Tutorial Program

Provides tutoring and homework assistance for students in grades 1 - 12 enrolled in Austin ISD. Students are matched on a 1:1 basis with community volunteers. The student/tutor pair meet a minimum of 1 hour per week. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1318355

Lone Star Legal Aid

Provides legal services for low-income individuals in certain civil cases only, no criminal or fee-generating cases are accepted. Assists with cases dealing with public benefits, housing assistance, landlord/tenant law, consumer law, family law, and rights for people with disabilities. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1171430

Manufactured Housing Division (MHD)

Licenses and regulates those who manufacture, sell, broker, and install manufactured homes to ensure that they are well-constructed and installed correctly, that consumers are provided fair and effective remedies, and that measures are taken to ensure economic stability for the Texas manufactured housing industry. Monitors manufacturers' performance in handling complaints, performs post-production monitoring, conducts training and issues licenses, state seals and statements of ownership and location (previously known as titles), performs installation inspections, and investigates consumer complaints. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1012496

Martin Middle School - Supplemental Educational Services (SES)

Provides services called Supplemental Educational Services under No Child Left Behind (NCLB). Provides extra help in academic subjects, such as reading, language arts and mathematics at no cost to eligible students. The services are provided outside of the regular school day either before school, after school or on weekends. They may be held at the school, in a program provider center, or at the student's home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1438544

Matched Savings Account

Provides a $3.00 to $1.00 matched savings account or Individual Development Accounts (IDAs)for individuals wishing to save money for higher education, purchasing a home, or investing in a small-business endeavor. For every $1.00 a person saves, the City will provide a $3.00 match. For example, if an individual saves $60.00, the City will match it with $180.00 for a total of $240.00 in your savings account. Limited funding is available for this program. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1380669

Mexican American Cultural Center (MACC)

Provides a cultural center dedicated to dedicated to the preservation, creation, presentation, and promotion of Mexican American cultural arts and heritage. The center is a resource for the community and visitors, youth and adults, to learn and participate in classes and programs that will foster understanding and appreciation of not only Mexican American but also Native American, Chicano, and other Latino cultures. The programs and educational curriculum include the areas of visual art, theater, dance, literature, music, multi-media and the culinary arts. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1306695

Mexic-arte Museum - Art Classes for Youth

Provides after-school and school-based art enrichment programs for youth who attend school in the Austin, Del Valle and Manor ISD. Mexic-Arte Museum classes provide youth with a supportive environment to learn new art skills that connect them to Mexic-Arte Museum exhibits. Classes also include a field trip to the Mexic-Arte Museum for a guided tour of the current exhibits. Summer and community-based programs are also offered at Southeast Branch of the Austin Public Library and River City Youth Foundation. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304801

Military OneSource - Information and Referral Hotline

Provides a 24-hour, 7 days a week, toll-free information and referral telephone service available worldwide to active duty, Reserve, and National Guard military members and their families; and to deployed civilians and their families. Military OneSource provides information ranging from everyday concerns to deployment-related issues. Also, if there is a need for face-to-face counseling, Military OneSource can provide a referral for six sessions per issue to professional civilian counselors at no cost to the service member or family member (please note in-person counseling is only available in the United States and Puerto Rico). Overseas, Military OneSource can help access the existing services provided through the Medical Treatment Facilities. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011592

Military Service

The official charity of the United States Air Force. Provides worldwide emergency assistance, sponsoring education assistance programs, and offers an array of base community enhancement programs that improve quality of life for Airmen and their families.Offers the following programs:Emergency Assistance:- Financial Assistance, Assistance to Reserve/GuardEducation Programs:- Grants, Spouse Tuition Assistance, Scholarship LinksCommunity Programs:- Give Parents a Break- Bundles for Babies- Car Care Because We Care- Child Care for PCS- Phone Home- Respite Care- Spouse Orientation Program- Spouse Employment Program- Child Care for Volunteers- Youth Employment Skills YES - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/982516

Military Service

Military Service

Offers:-Emergency Financial Aid-direct financial aid to soldiers and their families in crisis,-Family Support Network-concerts, sporting events, special outings to help reunite families, therapeutic day camp for children of wounded heroes and more,-Wounded Hero Career Network-programs that assist wounded Vets and their spouses in transition from their career in the military to exploring options in the civilian workplace,-Homes for Wounded Heroes-disability-adapted homes that are nearly cost-free for wheelchair-bound and blind veterans,-Road to Recovery Conference-all-expense paid educational and service event for wounded heroes and their families. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/982532

MILITARY SERVICE

Offers a mobile herd of trained, miniature horse ambassadors to visit adults and children in need. National Runaway Safeline

Provides crisis intervention, information and referral, message relay, conflict mediation, conference calling, home free (free bus tickets to reunify families through Greyhound bus lines for youth 12 - 20 who qualify), runaway education and prevention materials, Runaway Prevention Curriculum available free of charge, and web services such as crisis email, crisis bulletin board, national and state statistics, and online parent chat. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011908

National Runaway Safeline - Home Free Program

Provides free bus ticket for runaways to return home after meeting eligibility guidelines. When calling the switchboard number, staff will make a conference call between youth and the legal guardian, who will be asked for a copy of the runaway report. National Runaway Safeline will then contact Greyhound to make travel arrangements. Once home, staff will work with the parents and youth to rebuild their relationship, and will provide referrals to community resources. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/981807

National Safe Place

Safe Place is a national youth outreach program that educates thousands of young people every year about the dangers of running away or trying to resolve difficult, threatening situations on their own. This easily-replicated initiative involves the whole community to provide safe havens and resources for youth in crisis. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1343316

National Suicide Prevention Lifeline

Provides a 24-hour, toll-free suicide prevention service available to anyone in suicidal crisis. If you need help, please dial 800.273.TALK (8255). You will be routed to the closest possible crisis center in your area. With over 120 crisis centers across the country, our mission is to provide immediate assistance to anyone seeking mental health services. Call for yourself, or someone you care about. Your call is free and confidential. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1012061

NCFH - Call for Health Program

Provides nationwide information and referral to affordable, accessible health care for farmworkers and their families. May provide limited medical financial assistance for farmworkers with low income when a migrant health center is not available in the area, or if it cannot provide services, and if there are no other local resources available, including private and public insurance. Works to enhance the capacity of Migrant Health Centers (MHCs) in the US. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305331

Online Crime Reporting

Provides a web-based program that will allow citizens to file non-emergency, low priority reports, 24 hours a day, 7 days a week. Citizens will be provided with a copy of their report along with a temporary case number. The report will then be reviewed internally and the citizen will be notified if the report is approved or rejected for follow-up. The system will be further enhanced to accommodate business owners who have regular incidents such as shoplifting. Soon citizens will have the option to report crimes in other languages such as Spanish and possibly Vietnamese. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308842

Pasadena Office - DADS Adult Foster Care (AFC)

Adult Foster Care provides 24-hour living arrangement with supervision in an adult foster home for persons who, because of emotional, physical, or mental limitation, are unable to continue independent functioning in their own homes. Providers of AFC live in the household and share a common living area with individuals receiving services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428699

Pasadena Office - DADS Client Managed Personal Assistance Services (CMPAS)

DADS contracts with licensed agencies to provide personal assistance services to people who have physical disabilities who are mentally and emotionally competent and willing to supervise their attendant or have someone who can supervise the attendant for them. The individual interviews, selects, trains, supervises and releases their personal assistants. Pasadena Office - DADS Community Attendant Services (CAS)

Community Attendant Services (CAS) is a non-technical, non-skilled service providing in home attendant services to individuals with an approved medical need for assistance with personal care tasks. Pasadena Office - DADS Community Based Alternatives (CBA)

This program provides home- and community-based services to people who are elderly and to adults with disabilities as a cost-effective alternative to living in a nursing home. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. Services may be provided in a person's home or in a community-based living arrangement, such as a group home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1429165

Pasadena Office - DADS Community Living Assistance and Support Services (CLASS)

CLASS provides home- and community-based services to people with related conditions as a cost-effective alternative to placement in an intermediate care facility. This program is for individuals with an intellectual disability or a related condition (ICF/IID). A related condition is a disability, other than an intellectual disability, that originated before age 22 and that affects a person's ability to function in daily life. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428701

Pasadena Office - DADS Day Activity and Health Services (DAHS)

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428711

Pasadena Office - DADS Deaf Blind Multiple Disabilities Program (DBMD)

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. Pet Loss Support Group

For most people, a pet is more than just an animal, it is a member of the family. When a pet dies, is lost or stolen, or must be relinquished, it can be just as devastating as losing a loved one. Unfortunately, it can be difficult to speak with friends and family about the loss of a pet. All too often, pet owners are met with well-meaning attempts at minimizing the feeling of loss through the notion that, as animals, pets are easily replaceable. In order to help pet owners cope with their losses, the Houston SPCA offers the Pet Loss support group, a safe, supportive environment where thoughts and emotions can be shared with those of similar circumstances, and where feelings of grief are understood and validated. Pet Loss is facilitated by a licensed professional counselor specializing in grief, loss and crisis counseling. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239470

PetSafe

The PetSafe program allows families to flee from domestic abuse without being forced to abandon their much-loved pets to a violent or life-threatening environment. Through PetSafe, animals are given temporary boarding, veterinary care, vaccinations and spaying/neutering while their families work towards re-establishing a safe, stable life. PetSafe exists through a partnership between the Houston SPCA and local women and family shelters, such as the Houston Area Womens Center. By partnering with these shelters, we are able to help human and non-human family members escape from violence and possible death. A network of eighteen shelters sends referrals to the Houston SPCA, and once they arrive at our shelter, pets are given quality, loving care by an experienced staff. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239468

PUC - Critical Condition or Chronic Care Residential Disconnection Rule

Rule protects certain customers of retail electric providers and electric utilities from disconnection. Customers can be granted a "chronic condition" or "critical care" residential customer designation, but this does not relieve a customer of the obligation to pay the electric provided services and service continuity is still not guaranteed; electric cooperatives and municipally-owned electric utilities comply with the rule on a voluntary basis, and electricity may be disconnected for failure to pay. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1307657

PUC - Customer Questions/Complaints

Any affected person may complain to the PUC, either in writing or by telephone, in regards to their electric or telecommunication utility. Public Utility Commission staff may request a complaint made by telephone to be put in writing if necessary to complete the investigation. No form is required, but certain information is required (see Intake Requirements). - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1307655

PUC - Electric Service Deposit Waivers

Provides deposit waivers for victims of family violence and customers 65 years of age or older in a competitive electric area. See Eligibility and Intake for more information. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1424243

PUC - Lifeline

Helps qualified low-income individuals lower the cost of monthly home telephone service. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011895

PUC - Lifeline Support Cell Phone Providers

Lifeline provides support to telecommunications companies that offer free or low cost cell phones and cell phone service to eligible consumers. Consumers must enroll through one of the telecommunications companies. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1423001

PUC - Link-Up

Reduces the cost of installing new telephone service to qualifying low-income residents who live on approved tribal lands. Offers a 100% discount (up to $100) for telephone installation charges. Link-Up does not cover more than one phone line in the home, but the program does include an option for delaying payment on the balance of the connection fee, up to $200, for up to one year without interest charges. Link-Up does not offer financial assistance for additional services on the telephone, such as caller ID or voice messaging. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011172

PUC - Lite-Up Texas

The Lite-Up Texas Program is designed to help qualified low-income individuals reduce the monthly cost of electric service. Currently the program is providing an 82% discount for participants who register by April 10th, 2014, on all electric bills for service months May through August 2014, and 15% for September 2014. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011892

PUC Power to Choose - Texas Electric Choice

Texas Electric Choice is an education campaign created by the Public Utility Commission of Texas to inform Texans about electric competition and changes in the way you buy electricity. The state's electric market is open to competition, giving you the power of choice. This means that some Texans can choose their electricity provider. Website includes a search by zip code which helps to identify available area electrical providers in an area. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011894

PUC - Relay Texas (7-1-1)

Relay Texas provides confidential, telephone interpreting service between people who can hear and people who are deaf, hard of hearing, deaf-blind, or speech impaired. Either a TTY user or a person using a standard phone may initiate a call through Relay Texas by dialing the relay number 711 or the designated 10 digit number. After dialing Relay Texas, the person initiating the call gives the desired phone number to the Relay Texas Agent, who then dials that number using another phone line. The Relay Agent types the standard phone user's spoken words to the person using the TTY and voices the TTY user's text. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1307661

PUC - Texas Do Not Call List

By placing your name, address and telephone number on the Statewide Do Not Call List, you identify yourself as a consumer who does not wish to receive telemarketing calls. This list will be maintained by the Public Utility Commission of Texas (PUC). The list prevents telephone solicitations (including text messages or images) to residential and wireless phone numbers from all telemarketers operating in the state of Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1307660

RAINN - National Sexual Assault Hotline

Offers a free, confidential counseling and support hotline 24 hours a day for victims of sexual violence, their friends, and their families. Also provides an online hotline, which uses instant messaging to connect individuals with hotline staff. Automatically transfers callers to the rape crisis center nearest you, anywhere in the nation. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/982511

Rosenberg Office - DADS Adult Foster Care (AFC)

Adult Foster Care provides 24-hour living arrangement with supervision in an adult foster home for persons who, because of emotional, physical, or mental limitation, are unable to continue independent functioning in their own homes. Providers of AFC live in the household and share a common living area with individuals receiving services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428712

Rosenberg Office - DADS Assisted Living/Residential Care (AL/RC)

Assisted living facilities and adult residential care homes provide 24-hour supervision and non-medical attendant care for adults with disabilities. Eligible clients do not require nursing home care. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428715

Rosenberg Office - DADS Client Managed Personal Assistance Services (CMPAS)

DADS contracts with licensed agencies to provide personal assistance services to people who have physical disabilities who are mentally and emotionally competent and willing to supervise their attendant or have someone who can supervise the attendant for them. The individual interviews, selects, trains, supervises and releases their personal assistants. Health-related tasks are prescribed by physician. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428512

Rosenberg Office - DADS Community Attendant Services (CAS)

Community Attendant Services (CAS) is a non-technical, non-skilled service providing in home attendant services to individuals with an approved medical need for assistance with personal care tasks. CAS is available to eligible adults and children whose health problems cause them to be functionally limited in performing activities of daily living according to practitioner’s statement of medical need. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428714

Rosenberg Office - DADS Community Based Alternatives (CBA)

This program provides home- and community-based services to people who are elderly and to adults with disabilities as a cost-effective alternative to living in a nursing home. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. Services may be provided in a person's home or in a community-based living arrangement, such as a group home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1429166

Rosenberg Office - DADS Community Living Assistance and Support Services (CLASS)

CLASS provides home- and community-based services to people with related conditions as a cost-effective alternative to placement in an intermediate care facility. This program is for individuals with an intellectual disability or a related condition (ICF/IID). A related condition is a disability, other than an intellectual disability, that originated before age 22 and that affects a person's ability to function in daily life. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428713

Rosenberg Office - DADS Day Activity and Health Services (DAHS)

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428716

Rosenberg Office - DADS Deaf Blind Multiple Disabilities Program (DBMD)

This Medicaid- waiver program provides home and community-based services to people who are deaf-blind with multiple disabilities, as a cost-effective alternative to institutional placement. The program focuses on increasing opportunities for consumers to communicate and interact with their environment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428717

Rosenberg Office - DADS Emergency Response Services

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. In an emergency, the person can press a call button to signal for help. The electronic monitoring system helps to ensure that the appropriate person or service agency responds to an alarm call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428718

Rosenberg Office - DADS Family Care (FC)

Family Care (FC) is a non-skilled, non-technical attendant care service available to eligible adults who are functionally limited in performing activities of daily living. Family Care services are provided by an attendant and do not require the supervision of a registered nurse. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428719

Rosenberg Office - DADS Home-Delivered Meals (HDM)

The Home Delivered Meals program delivers at least one nutritious meal per day to individuals who are homebound and unable to prepare their own meals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428720

Rosenberg Office - DADS Hospice Care

A program of relieving care at an individual’s place of residence consisting of medical, social, and support services to a terminally ill patient when curative treatment is no longer possible. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428721

Rosenberg Office - DADS In Home and Family Support Services (IHFSP)

This program provides direct grant benefits to people who have physical disabilities, and/or to their families, to help them purchase services that enable them to live in the community. Participants choose and purchase services that help them to remain in their own homes. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428722

Rosenberg Office - DADS Medically Dependent Children Program (MDCP)

The program provides services to support families caring for children and young adults who are medically dependent and to encourage de-institutionalization of children in nursing facilities. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428723

Rosenberg Office - DADS Primary Home Care (PHC)

This program is a nontechnical, medically-related personal care service provided to adults whose health problems cause them to be functionally limited in performing activities of daily living, according to a statement of medical need. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428724

Services are provided by fully equipped mobile dental vans that travel between schools. Offers screenings, fillings, X-rays, sealants, general extractions, some root canals and cleanings. Pre-Kindergarten – 12th grade students at the listed Title 1 schools experiencing dental pain may receive emergency dental care. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1312959

Stuttering Foundation of America

The Stuttering Foundation provides free services and support to those who stutter and their families, as well as support for research into the causes of stuttering. We are the largest-and the first-nonprofit charitable organization in the world working toward the prevention and improved treatment of stuttering, reaching over a million people annually. We also offer extensive educational programs on stuttering for professionals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/989486

TAJF – Funding Services

Administers funds to legal aid organizations in order to provide civil legal services for people in Texas with low income. With TAJF grants, legal aid organizations provide free legal assistance to qualified individuals in civil matters, such as protection from domestic violence and assistance with housing issues. Collects and grants IOLTA funds (or the Texas Interest on Lawyers’ Trust Accounts Program). Offers links on website to legal information. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1314442

Talk Time is not a formal English as a Second Language ESL class. Participants must already speak some English to benefit. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1309467

Taxpayer Advocate Service (TAS)

Provides free, independent, impartial, and confidential tax assistance for individual and business taxpayers in resolving ongoing issues with the Internal Revenue Service (IRS) that have not been resolved through the normal processes. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1396294

Taxpayer Advocate Service (TAS) - Austin

Provides free, independent, impartial, and confidential tax assistance for individual and business taxpayers in resolving ongoing issues with the Internal Revenue Service (IRS) that have not been resolved through the normal processes. Assists taxpayers who are facing significant economic hardships, or will suffer significant hardship or costs if relief is not granted; taxpayers who experienced an IRS delay of more than 30 days to resolve a tax issue; or taxpayers who have not received a response or resolution to the problem by the date that was promised by the IRS. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1322920

TCEQ - Environmental Permits

TCEQ - Occupational Licensing

Licenses individuals whose occupations may have an environmental impact. The section’s duties include issuing new licenses, renewing licenses, training approval and exam development. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1454969

TCEQ Region 12 - Field Office

Serves as the environmental agency for Region 12. Responds to reports of environmental emergencies. Investigates complaints regarding air, land, or water pollution, or about people or companies licensed or registered by the TCEQ. Also provides assistance in understanding environmental laws. Provides a central registry of information about the sites, individuals, organizations, and entities the TCEQ regulates. Provides information on air and water quality, licensing, environmental cleanups, recycling, enforcement of environmental regulations, pending and completed environmental permits, and more. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1456359

TCEQ Region 12 - Small Business and Environmental Assistance

Provides confidential compliance assistance on air, water, and waste regulations to small businesses and small local governments; works with regulated entities, industries, and manufacturers to implement pollution prevention, recycling, and innovative environmental programs; and educates the public and the regulated community on rules, TCEQ processes, and environmental issues. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1454735

TCFV - Deaf Domestic Violence Hotline

Provides a national crisis intervention hotline offering information, support, and referrals to people in domestic violence situations or those calling on their behalf. Advocates who are Deaf are available from 11:00 am - 7:00 pm CST via: Videophone 855-812-1001; Instant Messenger (DeafHotline); or email (deafhelp@thehotline.org). - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980425

TCFV - National Domestic Violence Hotline

Provides national crisis intervention, information and referral to victims of domestic violence, perpetrators, friends and families. Advocates have access to information about more than 5,000 shelters and domestic violence programs across the US, Puerto Rico, the US Virgin Islands and Canada. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321206

TCFV - National Teen Dating Abuse Helpline Program (NTDAH)

Provides a 24-hour national web-based and telephone helpline for teens ages 13-18 experiencing dating abuse, and concerned parents, friends, teachers, clergy, law enforcement, and service providers. Helpline is staffed by trained Peer Advocates who provide information about the dynamics of relationship abuse and provide advocacy and support. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980420

TCFV - Public Awareness and Education

Promotes education regarding family violence. Provides support services to domestic violence agencies, including training and technical assistance for professionals, on-site program consultations, and legislative advocacy. Provides legislative update materials for domestic violence related laws. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980417

TCPA - Sales Tax Holiday

Provides an annual sales tax holiday on a Friday, Saturday, and Sunday of August (August 8th-10th for 2014) when no state or local sales taxes are charged on most clothing, footwear, and backpacks (for elementary and secondary students- not college students) priced under $100. Layaway plans may be used to take advantage of the sales tax holiday. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011270

TCPA - State Tax Collection Agencies

Collects taxes and fees owed the state and recommends ways of streamlining state government and making it smaller, smarter and faster. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/982497

TCPA - Tax Seminars

The Texas Comptroller's office offers sales & use tax seminars for business owners across the state throughout the year. New taxpayers are especially encouraged to attend these overviews of tax responsibilities for buyers, sellers, and service providers. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304860

TCPA - Texas Guaranteed Tuition Plan

The Texas Guaranteed Tuition Plan allows parents or organizations to prepay a child's college tuition at the current year's cost. A prepaid tuition contract can pay up to 160 credit hours of tuition and required fees for students at any public college or university or the estimated average private tuition and required fees for students at any private university. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304856

TCPA - Texas Safeguard

Provides an informational website and hotline for individuals that may have been included in an unintentional exposure of personal information in Spring, 2011. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1011691

TCPA - Texas Unclaimed Property Program

The Texas unclaimed property law requires financial institutions, businesses, and government entities to report to the state any individual's personal property they are holding that is considered abandoned or unclaimed. Property is turned over to the Comptroller's office annually when the owner's whereabouts are unknown and the property has been inactive on the books of the reporting company, after the appropriate abandonment period has passed. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/982494

TCRP - Legal Services

Provides direct legal representation, community education, public awareness campaigns, education and advocacy on behalf of those who have historically been under-served or excluded from the justice system because of socioeconomic status, ethnic background, race, immigration status, or lack of access to civil rights attorneys. When possible, provides referrals for individuals who cannot be directly assisted. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304864

TCRP - Violence Against Women Act (VAWA), Economic Justice Program (EJP)

Provides Civil rights litigation and ensure people with disabilities have equal access to facilities across Texas. Represents and educates people whose rights have been violated by predatory lenders, consumer rights, individuals violated by law enforcement and racial profiling, advocates for free speech, fair housing and title IX gender equity in sports and opportunities in high school for young women suffering physical, sexual and psychological abuse from their U.S. citizen or legal permanent resident spouses; emphasis in recovering underpaid or non-paid wages and fights against other labor rights violations. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428420

TDA - Texas Donated Dental Services (TXDDS)

Provides dental services for people who are over the age of 62 or have a permanent disability. The program maintains a waiting list and does not provide emergency care. All counties may not be taking applications for assistance, visit website or call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1317887

TDA - Texas Mission of Mercy (TMOM)

Offers annual multi-day events providing free dental care services to people in need. Formerly called Smiles on Wheels. Hundreds of dentists, dental professionals, and other volunteers from across Texas donate their professional services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1317888

TDCJ - Baby and Mother Bonding Initiative (BAMBI)

This initiative allows time to form a healthy attachment in a secure setting with a strong training and parenting education program for the mother, who will also receive child development, life skills, infant first aid and CPR, health and nutrition, and substance abuse education. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449718

TDCJ - Community Supervision and Corrections (Probation) Departments (CSCD)

CSCDs supervise and help rehabilitate offenders who are sentenced to community supervision by local courts. Supervision officers assess each offender's risk/needs and use the results to design an appropriate supervision plan. Some offenders are confined temporarily in residential facilities. Others are not confined, but must report to their community supervision officers at intervals determined by the courts. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449702

TDCJ - Correctional Institution Unit Directory

Website contains a directory of all correctional institutions located in the state of Texas. Unit names are given, along with unit codes, operating agency, facility type, TDCJ Region, and county. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449710

TDCJ - Crime Victim Clearinghouse (TXCVC)

Serves as a central source of information about services and issues involving crime victims in Texas. Through its toll-free number (800) 848-4284, the TxCVC helps connect victims with community and state resources throughout the state. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1172663

TDCJ - Drug and Alcohol Testing Program

Provides a program used to identify substance abusers, refer them to appropriate treatment programs, and monitor their progress. When an offender tests positive on one or more occasions, parole officers can take several actions immediately or recommend the Board of Pardons and Parolees impose sanctions. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310222

TDCJ - Electronic Monitoring Program

Provides electric monitoring augmentations of a releasee by electronically detecting curfew and home confinement violations. Also provides an alternative to revocation for those not responding to other forms of supervision. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310247

TDCJ - Evacuation Instruction for Offenders on Parole

During disasters in which state parole offenders are evacuating from their homes, they must call TDCJ at 866-680-6667 to report where they will be evacuting to. Parolees will need their State/Government-issued identification when they call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310258

TDCJ - Field Referral Program

Provides the Field Referral Program that targets the offenders who are on parole and have not participated in an In-Prison Therapeutic Community (IPTC) or Substance Abuse Felony Punishment Facility (SAFPF), but are in need of substance abuse treatment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310253

TDCJ - In-Prison Driving While Intoxicated (DWI) Recovery Program

A multimodal six month program developed for a complex population with diverse anti-social behavior issues and re-offending risk factors. The substance abuse treatment programming specifically targets those offenders who are incarcerated for a DWI offense. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449719

TDCJ - Mentally Ill Offender Program

Program combines specialized intensive supervision with community-based treatment services for offenders with severe and persistent mental disorders who are paroled or released to mandatory supervision. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310246

TDCJ - Offender Locator

Provides information about the status of an inmate in the Texas Criminal Justice system. Callers need to know the inmate's 7-digit Texas Department of Criminal Justice number, or know the inmate's full name, date of birth or approximate age, and county of conviction. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1172661

TDCJ - Offender Parole Status LIne

Provides information about the status of a parolee in the Texas Criminal Justice system. Callers need to know the inmate's Texas Department of Criminal Justice or State ID (SID) number. Inquiries can also be made via e-mail or website. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1172662

TDCJ Parole Division - Rosenberg

Supervision is provided for criminal offenders adult paroled from state correctional institutions who reside in the Houston Metropolitan area Harris County in an attempt to minimize parolees problems of returning to society, as well as social protection by crime prevention. The method of operation can be described as casework in a law enforcement setting. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1245140

TDCJ - Project Reintegration of Offenders

Provides a program that seeks to secure employment for offenders and thereby reduce recidivism. Parole officers refer unemployed, part-time employed, or underemployed offenders to a wide range of TWC/RIO employment assistance services in approximately 100 TWC offices statewide. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310242

TDCJ - Reentry Program

Voluntary reentry program that is offered on multiple units within the Texas Department of Criminal Justice. This program assists offenders in preparing for a successful return to the community. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449714

TDCJ - Sex Offender Rehabilitation Programs

Sex Offender Education Program (SOEP) consists of a four-month curriculum to assist sex offenders determined to pose a lower re-offense risk or who may be releasing to a lengthy term of supervision. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449720

TDCJ - Special Needs Program (SNP)

Program provides for the early parole of certain categories of offenders who have a mental illness, mental retardation, a terminal illness or physical disability, or who are elderly. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310240

TDCJ - State Headquarters

State agency operates state prisons, state jails, parole, and provides funding and certain oversight of community supervision previously known as adult probation. TDCJ primarily supervises adult offenders persons 17 or older assigned to state supervision. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321632

TDCJ - Substance Abuse Treatment Program

Substance Abuse Felony Punishment Facilities (SAFPFs) and In-Prison Therapeutic Communities (IPTCs) provide services to eligible offenders identified as needing substance abuse treatment. Both are 6-month in-prison treatment programs followed by up to 3 months of residential aftercare in a transitional treatment center (TTC) (see Helpful Tips), 6 to 9 months of outpatient aftercare, and up to 12 months of support groups and follow-up supervision. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449722

TDCJ - Super-Intensive Supervision Program (SISP)

Provides the highest level of supervision and offender accountability to releasees supervised by TDCJ Parole Division. All SISP offenders are supervised on some from of electronic monitoring and are required to comply with 24-hour-a-day schedules approved in advance by their parole officer. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310235

TDCJ - Therapuetic Community Program (TCP)

Program targets offenders who have participated in the In-Prison Therapeutic Community (IPTC) or Substance Abuse Felony Punishment (SAFPF) facility programs. The continuum of care plan begins during incarceration in the IPTC or SAFPF and continues immediately upon release to parole or mandatory supervision. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310230

TDCJ - Victim Notification System

The Victim Notification System (VNS) utilizes a confidential database to provide registrants with notifications regarding offender(s). Notifications are available via email, letter or both. The system provides over 80 points of possible notification, regarding several phases of an offender’s incarceration and the parole review process. Once an individual is added to the VNS, they will receive a confirmation letter with two brochures that further explain services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1172664

TDCJ - Victim Services

Through victim interviews, produces the Victim Impact Statement which is included in the pre-sentence investigation report for the court's information and assistance in determining sentencing and appropriate restitution. Staff members accompany victims to court proceedings when support is needed. This office provides information to victims inquiries regarding restitution and general status of the defendants supervision. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1258503

TDCJ - Voice Monitoring Program (VMP)

A passive monitoring system that has the ability to randomly call releasees' pagers, who then call a predetermined number, where their voice pattern is identified and their location verified. A voice print of each releasee is maintained by the VMP vendor. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1310224

TDCJ - Volunteer Services

Volunteers assist in providing literacy and educational programs, life skills training, job skills training, parent-training, medical issues and prevention training, arts and crafts programs, drug and alcohol rehabilitation programs, faith-based programming, and other programs determined by TDCJ to aid in the transition between confinement and society and to reduce incidence of recidivism. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1449716

TDI - Auto Market Assistance Program

Links good drivers who live in designated areas with auto insurers that will consider them for coverage at rates lower than what they may now be paying. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321871

TDI - Consumer Protection Program

Accepts and investigates complaints against insurance companies, HMOs, insurance agents, adjusters, and fully insured or fully funded health benefit plans. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321875

TDI - Consumer Services

Provides general information, online or by calling, about various types of insurance, including health, auto, home, life, long-term, and commercial. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321874

TDI - Division of Workers' Compensation

Provides assistance with workers' compensation claims. Workers' compensation provides covered employees with income and medical benefits if they are injured on the job or have a work-related injury or illness. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321885

TDI - Home Market Assistance Program

Assists homeowners and renters who have been unable to find insurance for their houses, mobile homes, or apartments with participating insurance companies. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321876

TDI - Insurance Fraud Unit

Investigates complaints about entities selling insurance without a license, which is a felony in Texas. The public may verify company licenses and agent licenses online or by calling the Consumer Help Line at 800-252-3439. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321878

TDI - Office of Injured Employee Counsel (OIEC)

Unrepresented injured workers may be assisted by an ombudsman through the OIEC. Service is free of charge to workers who have disputes with workers' compensation claims. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/991101

TDI - State Fire Marshal's Office (SFMO)

Provides assistance to local authorities in the investigation of suspected arson and burn ban violators. Services include the use of the state's Forensic Arson Laboratory. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321881

TDI - Texas Consumer Health Assistance Program (CHAP)

Texas CHAP is operated by the Texas Department of Insurance to help Texas consumers with health insurance issues. Texas CHAP is part of a network of state consumer assistance programs funded by the U.S. Department of Health and Human Services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321883

TDI - Texas State Continuation Plan

Provides information about COBRA insurance and the Texas State Continuation Plan. This program may allow you to continue coverage for an additional six months after your COBRA coverage ends. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1321877

TDLR - Licensing, Certification and Accreditation

Regulates over twenty types of businesses, industries, trades, and occupations. Issues licenses, conducts inspections, investigates complaints, assesses penalties, sets rules and standards, and holds hearings. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/982584

Teacher Retirement System of Texas - Services

Provides retirement and related benefits for people employed by the public schools, colleges, and universities supported by the State of Texas. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1315351

TEA - GED Records Request

Maintains GED test records, issues duplicate certificates and transcripts, and issues equivalency certificates to qualified candidates. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305538

TEA - General Education Development Test (GED)

Provides eligible candidates the opportunity to earn high school equivalency credentials. Test covers 5 subjects: Mathematics, Science, Social Studies, Writing Skills, and Interpreting Literature and the Arts. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305543

TEA - Parents Special Education Information Line

Provides information to assist parents with special education concerns in public schools in Texas. Parents can ask questions about student rights, possible violations of those rights, and regulatory requirements as they relate to special education complaint investigations, mediation, and due process hearings. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1305542

TEA - School Closure Information

Website which lists school closings/delays in the event of weather or other issues. The list is updated several times daily. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1447751

TEA - School District Locator

The TEA School District Locator tool is an up-to-date, accurate map tool to locate school districts or individual schools. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1343288

Teen Dating Relationship Education

Provides teen dating relationship education to help prevent dating violence. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239769

Texans Standing Tall - Community Services

Provides information, resources, training, and technical assistance on preventing underage alcohol, tobacco, and other drug use. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1304813

Texas Advocacy Project - Family Law Hotline Services

Provides free legal advice related to family law in the areas of divorce, child custody/visitation, child support and orders of protection. Callers will speak with an intake specialist who will determine services needed. A staff attorney will contact the caller within 3-5 business days. Callers may be referred to attorneys or agencies for free consultation or representation. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980793

Texas Advocacy Project - Family Violence and Sexual Assault Legal Lines

Provides free legal advice for victims of family violence or sexual abuse in the areas of family law, divorce, child custody, financial support and dating violence. Callers will be contacted by a staff attorney within 3-5 business days and may be referred to an attorney or agency for free consultation or representation. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980796

Provides assistance with safety plans, shelter locations and options for domestic violence victims. Services may include assistance in obtaining protective orders and help with Crime Victim's Compensation claims. Assists with completion of application forms, appeals, and expedited processing for emergency funds. Callers will be contacted by a technical advocate in 3-5 business days. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980785

Receives new hire information from employers and tracks employment information on child support obligors.New Hire Reporting is mandated by federal law under the Personal Responsibility and Work Opportunity Reconciliation Act of 1996, and requires employers to report new hires and rehires within 20 calendar days. Information received from employers is entered into a statewide registry and then transmitted to the National Directory of New Hires. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/989844

Texas Attorney General - Identity Theft Victim Resources

*Target Corporation has announced a breach of its point-of-sale system, resulting in the credit/debit card information of 40 million customers being compromised. Customers who shopped at Target store locations between November 27th and December 15th, 2013 may be at risk. These customers are advised to check their bank statements carefully for any unexplained charges. Victims should take steps to mitigate further losses, and immediately file a report with their local law enforcement agencies. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1446426

Texas Attorney General - State Attorneys General

Issues rulings and decisions that determine whether information is open to the public under the Public Information Act and other applicable laws. The division hotline can answer questions regarding the laws and help resolve disputes involving the open government laws. Also includes freedom of information requests. However, the hotline cannot provide legal advice to private citizens or governmental entities.Any information collected, assembled, or maintained by or for a governmental body is subject to the Public Information Act. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980265

Texas Attorney General - Texas Access and Visitation Hotline

The Texas Access and Visitation Hotline provides noncustodial and custodial parents with free phone access to attorneys who provide legal information and assistance related to child custody and visitation issues, as well as paternity and child support information. Hotline attorneys do not represent parents. They provide explanations of legal orders, provide tools and guidance for resolution of child access issues, and answer parents' questions regarding possession and access orders, custody, paternity and child support.The hotline has a corresponding website, www.txaccess.org, where parents can download sample materials and tools for assistance with child access issues. Additional brief legal coaching or self-help assistance may be available to eligible Hotline callers. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1322433

Texas Attorney General - Texas Vine

Provides a 24-hour, bilingual hotline giving basic information on jailed offenders, case information, and scheduled court events. Notifies registered users such as crime victims of changes in court status and when an offender is released, transferred, or has escaped.Information provided about an offender: name of offender/alias, ID number, date of birth, current custody status, location, sentence expiration date, scheduled release date, charges, bail, and court event information.Sponsored by the Texas Office of Attorney General, Office of the Governor, and local county officials. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1322436

Texas Baptist Children’s Home - Campus Life Program

Provides 24-hour residential care in a family-like environment for children who are experiencing a family crisis, such as alcohol or substance abuse, violence, family disruption due to divorce, death, unemployment, incarceration or other issues leading to family conflict. Minimum length of stay is 6 months. Children attend public school in the Round Rock ISD. Provides individual, group, and play therapy as needed.Families are encouraged to participate in planning their child's care and future. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308152

Texas Baptist Children’s Home - Family Care Program

Provides transitional housing for single mothers and their children. Services include case management, individual and group counseling, goal setting, budgeting, parenting, homemaking, spiritual growth, and relationship building. Residents must commit to being gainfully employed and saving toward future stability. Each unit has bedroom, bathroom, and kitchen areas, and families share large dining, living, laundry, and play spaces. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308156

Texas BootStrap Loan Program

Works with nonprofit organizations to promote and enhance homeownership for people with low income by providing loan funds to purchase or refinance property on which clients may build new or improve existing residential housing. All participants must provide at least 65% sweat equity on their homes that is necessary to construct or rehabilitate the home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/980357

Texas City Office - DADS Adult Foster Care (AFC)

Adult Foster Care provides 24-hour living arrangement with supervision in an adult foster home for persons who, because of emotional, physical, or mental limitation, are unable to continue independent functioning in their own homes. Providers of AFC live in the household and share a common living area with individuals receiving services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428725

Texas City Office - DADS Assisted Living/Residential Care (AL/RC)

Assisted living facilities and adult residential care homes provide 24-hour supervision and non-medical attendant care for adults with disabilities. Eligible clients do not require nursing home care. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428726

Texas City Office - DADS Community Attendant Services (CAS)

Community Attendant Services (CAS) is a non-technical, non-skilled service providing in home attendant services to individuals with an approved medical need for assistance with personal care tasks. CAS is available to eligible adults and children whose health problems cause them to be functionally limited in performing activities of daily living according to practitioner’s statement of medical need. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428728

Texas City Office - DADS Community Based Alternatives (CBA)

This program provides home- and community-based services to people who are elderly and to adults with disabilities as a cost-effective alternative to living in a nursing home. Texas Department of Aging and Disability Services employees provide case management services. Services may be provided in a person's home or in a community-based living arrangement, such as a group home. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1429167

Texas City Office - DADS Community Living Assistance and Support Services (CLASS)

CLASS provides home- and community-based services to people with related conditions as a cost-effective alternative to placement in an intermediate care facility. This program is for individuals with an intellectual disability or a related condition (ICF/IID). A related condition is a disability, other than an intellectual disability, that originated before age 22 and that affects a person's ability to function in daily life. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428727

Texas City Office - DADS Day Activity and Health Services (DAHS)

Licensed day activity and health services (DAHS) facilities provide daytime services to people who live in the community as an alternative to living in a nursing home or other institution. Services, which usually are provided Monday through Friday, address physical, mental, medical and social needs. Sometimes, this is called adult day care or adult day services. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428729

Texas City Office - DADS Deaf Blind Multiple Disabilities Program (DBMD)

This Medicaid- waiver program provides home and community-based services to people who are deaf-blind with multiple disabilities, as a cost-effective alternative to institutional placement. The program focuses on increasing opportunities for consumers to communicate and interact with their environment. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428730

Texas City Office - DADS Emergency Response Services

Emergency response services are provided through an electronic monitoring system that is used by functionally impaired adults who live alone or who are socially isolated in the community. In an emergency, the person can press a call button to signal for help. The electronic monitoring system helps to ensure that the appropriate person or service agency responds to an alarm call. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428731

Texas City Office - DADS Family Care (FC)

Family Care (FC) is a non-skilled, non-technical attendant care service available to eligible adults who are functionally limited in performing activities of daily living. Family Care services are provided by an attendant and do not require the supervision of a registered nurse. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428732

Texas City Office - DADS Home-Delivered Meals (HDM)

The Home Delivered Meals program delivers at least one nutritious meal per day to individuals who are homebound and unable to prepare their own meals. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428733

Texas City Office - DADS Hospice Care

A program of relieving care at an individual’s place of residence consisting of medical, social, and support services to a terminally ill patient when curative treatment is no longer possible. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428734

Texas City Office - DADS In Home and Family Support Services (IHFSP)

This program provides direct grant benefits to people who have physical disabilities, and/or to their families, to help them purchase services that enable them to live in the community. Participants choose and purchase services that help them to remain in their own homes. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1428735

Texas Facilities Commission - State Surplus Property Program

Administers the state of Texas' surplus property program. When a Texas state agency has surplus property, the property is posted on the Comptroller's website for 10 business days. During that 10-day period, only qualified entities may obtain the property from state agencies. After the 10-day period, the public is eligible to purchase the property at one of three storefronts. The type of surplus property available ranges from abandoned airport property, to retired DPS vehicles, to TxDOT heavy equipment and all types of office furniture. Assistance organizations interested in obtaining surplus property are required to apply for program eligibility with TFC. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1436498

Vehicle Identification Number (VINE) Etching Program

Provides free permanent etching of the Vehicle Identification Number on the windows of vehicles. If the vehicle is stolen, the windows will need to be replaced before it can be sold. Because VIN etching is a permanent theft deterrent device, many insurance companies will give a discount to car owners who use this program. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308788

Sea Scouts are Venturers with a special interest in aquatic activities. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1243400

Volunteer Services

The Houston SPCA would not be able to provide so many services to Houstons animals and pet owners were it not for the dedication of our volunteers. We are able to operate thanks to the hard work of an extensive network of over 600 volunteers, who provide direct assistance to our programs and shelter operations. Volunteers may assist potential adopters in the shelter, and they can also work directly with the animals. Our volunteers help our staff to feed, water and clean up after the many animals in our careboth at the main shelter and at our barns. They also help walk dogs and socialize/train animals. Our foster care program is run entirely on volunteers. Houston SPCA volunteers from the community provided foster care to over 1,500 dogs, cats, puppies, kittens and other animals that were too young, sick, injured or simply in need of a break from shelter life. Volunteers from the Junior League of Houston operate our Pet Therapy program and take Houston SPCA companion animals to visit local retirement homes weekly. Our volunteers also assist in the weeklong Critter Camp program, which is offered in the summer and over the holidays. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1239469

Volunteers in Police Services (VIPS)

Trains volunteers to work in a number of capacities throughout the Austin Police Department. Some are graduates of the Citizens Police Academy who, among other things, participate in the practical exercises with all cadet classes. There are over 60 VIPs who write citations to people who park illegally in disabled parking spaces. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/1308812

Wellness Programs

Programs that offer individual and/or group sessions which assist participants to understand how their lifestyle impacts their physical and mental health and to develop personal practices that enhance their total well-being. Wellness programs are holistic and combine a variety of components which may include a general physical examination that is tailored to the individual's needs; an evaluation of the person's pattern of exercise, eating habits, sources of stress and other lifestyle elements that are potential risk factors; and the development and implementation of an individualized plan for prevention management and early intervention to optimize health and performance which may include physical fitness sessions, nutrition counseling, stress reduction techniques, biofeedback, practice in assuming responsibility for one's choices, and other specific measures for avoiding physical and mental health problems. - https://www.211texas.org/zf/profile/service/id/991099

A bank with branches in Austin that accepts the matricula consular card for Mexican nationals as an acceptable form of photo identification for opening a depository bank account.
